\DoxyCodeLine{07382\ TEST(ArrayEqTest,\ WorksForOneDimensionalArrays)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{07383\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Note\ that\ a\ and\ b\ are\ distinct\ but\ compatible\ types.}}
